###Return all the cases where the vaccine recipient got MENB or PNEUMONIA.
Answer:
{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""should"": [
                {
                    ""match"": {
                        ""SYMPTOM_TEXT"": ""MENB""
                    }
                },
                {
                    ""match"": {
                        ""SYMPTOM_TEXT"": ""PNEUMONIA""
                    }
                }
            ],
            ""minimum_should_match"": 1,
            ""filter"": [
                {
                    ""match"": {
                        ""DIED"": ""0""
                    }
                }
            ]"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        [
            {
                ""host"": ""localhost"",
                ""port"": 9200,
            }
        ]
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body={""query"": {""match"": {""STATE"": ""LA""}}})
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % len(res[""hits""][""hits""]))
    for hit in res[""hits""][""hits""]:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])

from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt


def get_data(es):
    # Get data from ES
    res = es.search(index=""vaers-2013"", body={""query"": {""match_all"": {}}})

    # Create dataframe from hits
    df = pd.DataFrame([doc[""_source""] for doc in res[""hits""][""hits""]])
    
    return df

def get_question(text):
    return text[:text.find(""###"")]


def get_answer(text):
    return text[text.find(""###"") + 3 :].strip()


def get_prompt(text):
    prompt = """"
    if ""Prompt:"" in text:
        prompt += text[text.find(""Prompt:"") :]

    if ""Clinical Notes:"" in text:
        prompt += ""\n"" + text[text.find(""Clinical Notes:"") :]

    return prompt.replace(""\n"", """")


def get_field_name(text):
    return text[text.find(""### "") + 4 : text.find(""### "", text.find(""### "") + 5)].strip()


def get_condition_value(text):
    return text[text.find(""###"

    """"""

    return [hit['_source'] for hit in res['hits']['hits']]

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        # Connect to local elasticsearch instance
        es = Elasticsearch()
    except Exception as e:
        print(""Connection failed"")
        sys.exit(1)

    return es

def get_condition(question):
    '''
    This function extracts the condition value from the question string. 
    The condition value is in between square brackets.
    '''
    # Find the index of the first left bracket ""[""
    start = question.find(""["") + 1
    
    # Find the index of the last right bracket ""]""
    end = question.rfind(""]"")

    return question[start : end]

def get_vax_name(text):
    if 'Zoster' in text or 'zoster' in text:
        return '<NAME>'
    elif 'DTaP' in text or 'dtap' in text:
        return 'DTaP'
    elif 'Hepatitis B' in text or 'hepatitis b' in text:
        return 'HEPB'
    else:"

def get_condition(question):
    """"""
    Get the condition from the question.

    Args:
        question (str): The question string.

    Returns:
        str: The condition string.
    """"""
    return re.search(""### ([^#]+)###"", question).group(1)


def get_field_name(question):
    """"""
    Get the field name from the question.

    Args:
        question (str): The question string.

    Returns:
        str: The field name string.
    """"""
    return re.search(""### [^#]+### ([^#]+)###"", question).group(1)

    """"""
    Get the condition value from the question.

    Args:
        question (str"

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])
        if not es.ping():
            raise ConnectionError(""Elasticsearch service unavailable"")
    except Exception as e:
        print(e)

    return es

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def get_data(index):
    """"""
    This function will return all data from an index of ElasticSearch
    :param index: The name of the index you want to search
    :return: All documents from that index
    """"""

    # Get all documents from the index
    res = es.search(
        index=index,
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match_all"": {}
            }
        },
        size=10000)

    # Return all documents
    return res['hits']['hits']

    """"""
    This function will return all data from an index

    :param index: The index you want to search
    :return: All documents from that index
    """"""
    res = es.search(
        index=index,
        body={
            ""query"": {
                ""match_all"": {}
            }
        },
        size=10000)
    return res['hits']['hits']

def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es

def test_extract_field():
    assert extract_field(
        ""RECVDATE"", ""Elasticsearch database with field names:""

def get_es_client():
    es = None
    try:
        es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])
        if not es.ping():
            raise ConnectionError(""Elasticsearch service unavailable"")
    except Exception as e:
        print(e)

    return es


def search_by_field_value(es, index, field_name, field_value):
    # Search by field"

def get_symptom(text):
    symptoms = []
    text = re.sub('[^A-Za-z0-9]+','', text)
    tokens = nltk.word_tokenize(text)
    pos = nltk.pos_tag(tokens)
    for i in range(len(pos)):
        if (pos[i][1] == 'NN' or pos[i][1] == 'NNS') and len(pos[i][0]) > 2:
            symptoms.append(pos[i][0].lower())
    return list(set"

        }
    }

def get_condition(field):
    if field == 'RECVDATE':
        return '2021-03-01'
    elif field == 'STATE':
        return 'VA'
    else:
        return ''


def generate_elasticsearch_query(field, condition):
    if field in ['RECVDATE', 'STATE']:
        return {""match"": {field: condition}}

    elif field == 'AGE_YRS':
        return {""range"": {'AGE_YRS': {'gte': int(condition), 'lte': int(condition)}}}
    
    elif field == 'VAERS_"

2130,"###How to generate the Elasticsearch query?
###Execute the Elasticsearch query and get the result.
###Print out the results in a table format.

""""""
import requests
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def search(index=""vaersdata"", body=None):
    if not es.indices.exists(index=index):
        return ""Index does not exist""

    res = es.search(index=index, body=body)
    hits = res[""hits""][""total""]
    print(""Total Hits:"", hits)
    return [hit['_source'] for hit in res['hits']['hits']]

import requests
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch
es = Elasticsearch()


def search(index=""vaersdata"", body=None):
    if not es.indices.exists(index=index):
        return ""Index does not exist""

    res = es.search(index=index, body=body)
    hits = res[""hits""][""total""]
    print(""Total Hits:"", hits)
    return [hit['_source'] for hit in res['hits']['hits']]

def get_data(index):
    """"""
    This function gets data from an index in Elasticsearch

    Parameters
    ----------
    index : str
        The name of the index you want to search
    
    Returns
    -------
    dict
        Dictionary containing all documents from the specified index
    """"""
    res = es.search(index=index)
    return res['hits']['hits']

5114,"###How to generate the Elasticsearch query?
###How to get the result of the query?
###How to display the result in the chatbot?
""""""


def test_es_query():
    assert es_query(""VAERS"", ""K"") == {
        'query': {'match': {'K': 'K'}}}

    assert es_query(""VAERS"", ""K"", ""A"") == {
        'query': {'bool': {'must': [{'match': {'K': 'K'}},
                                    {'match': {'A': 'A'}}]}}}

    assert es_query(""VAERS"", ""K"", ""A"", ""B"") == {
        'query': {'bool': {'must': [{'match': {'K': 'K'}},
                                    {'match': {'A': 'A'}},
                                    {'match': {'B': 'B'}}]}}}

    assert es_query(""VAERS"", ""K"", ""A"", ""B"","

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        [
            {
                ""host"": ""localhost"",
                ""port"": 9200,
            }
        ]
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_value(es, index, field_name, field_value):
    body = {""query"": {""match"": {field_name: field_value}}}
    res = es.search(index=index, body=body)
    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res[""hits""][""total""][""value""])
    for hit in res[""hits""][""hits""]:
        # print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)"

    assert extract_field(""SYMPTOM_TEXT"") == ""symptom_text"", \

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        [
            {
                ""host"": ""localhost"",
                ""port"": 9200,
            }
        ]
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):
    # Search by field name
    print(""Search by field name"")
    body = {""query"": {""match"": {""STATE"": ""TX""}}}
    res = es.search(index=""vaersdata"", body=body)
    print(json.dumps(res, indent=4))

    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_name(es):

                    ""_source"": [""RECVDATE""],
                    ""query"": {
                        ""match_all"": {}"

from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch(
        hosts=[{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}],
        http_auth=('elastic', '<PASSWORD>'),
        scheme=""https"",
        retry_on_timeout=True,
        max_retries=10
    )

    return es


def search_by_field_value(es):

        }
    })

        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text"

import json
from elasticsearch import Elasticsearch


def get_es():
    es = Elasticsearch([{'host': 'localhost', 'port': 9200}])
    return es


def search(es):
    # Search for a document by id
    res = es.get(index=""vaers"", doc_type=""_doc"", id=1)

    print(""Got %d Hits:"" % res['hits']['total'])
    for hit in res['hits']['hits']:
        print(""%(timestamp)s %(author)s: %(text)s"" % hit[""_source""])


if __name__ == '__main__':
    es = get_es()
    search(es)"

                        }
                    }
                },
                {

                        ""field"": ""HOSPITAL""
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    }
